## <a name="windows-server-2012-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="49579-2164">Attributi di Windows Server 2012</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49579-2164">Windows Server 2012 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49579-2165">Questa classe contiene gli attributi seguenti per Windows Server 2012:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49579-2165">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2012:</span></span>
